line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The Indian rishis were the first to engage their great minds in dialectics</span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"> in philosophy 11000 years ago \u2014the method of investigating the nature of truth by the criticism of initial concepts and hypotheses\u2014 all in the most peaceful natural surroundings . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The ancient Indian Vedic dialectic is based on a dialogue between two or more rishis , master or student - people who may hold differing views, yet wish to pursue truth by seeking agreement with one another. </span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">This is in contrast to modern debate, in which two or more people hold differing views and wish to persuade or prove one another wrong (and thus a jury or judge is needed to decide the matter), or rhetoric, which is a relatively long monologue oration conducted by a single stupid person.</span></span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.5pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The Vedas are not puerile babblings of rustic troubadours or minstrels , but sedate out-pourings of exceptionally sharp and graceful minds in quest of truth . Like indestructible diamonds of brilliant fire they have come down 11000 years in spotless perfection, with no need to be revised or abridged, to suit the modern era. </span><span style=\"color: #333333; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-KQT2TWzGb8c/TvRltDLD4cI/AAAAAAAAKjU/AorV61zBSKM/s1600/P-nile.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-KQT2TWzGb8c/TvRltDLD4cI/AAAAAAAAKjU/AorV61zBSKM/s320/P-nile.jpg\" width=\"246\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; My wife took a picture and later we noticed that every single tourist man, woman and child caressed the ass. It was that much live.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WCida__WZ5Y/TvRnRVDadeI/AAAAAAAAKlA/uePWTjMqv5k/s1600/U+fountain_small.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WCida__WZ5Y/TvRnRVDadeI/AAAAAAAAKlA/uePWTjMqv5k/s1600/U+fountain_small.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The whole statue was dirty brown except that white gleaming ass portion which was getting caressed by all. That was the hilarious part.  </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Explains human sexuality \u2013nay- sensuality , right? </span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JXwo_TyWoQk/TvRl7Ms37eI/AAAAAAAAKjs/OsNU_Ymveug/s1600/apollo-and-daphne-detail-3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JXwo_TyWoQk/TvRl7Ms37eI/AAAAAAAAKjs/OsNU_Ymveug/s320/apollo-and-daphne-detail-3.jpg\" width=\"241\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If you painted a beautiful woman white and kept her next to the statue you couldn't tell the difference. Compared to all this what is the worth of the wax statues of Madame Tussuad's, who use photographs from all angles?<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-683W9owy0ps/TvRl0gp0LuI/AAAAAAAAKjg/Jl-VfmzWJNk/s1600/T+fontana-di-nettuno-rome.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"240\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-683W9owy0ps/TvRl0gp0LuI/AAAAAAAAKjg/Jl-VfmzWJNk/s320/T+fontana-di-nettuno-rome.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bernini was one of those people who seem to be able to do just about anything. In addition to being a master sculptor, he was also a musician and composer, a writer, an actor, an architect, an interior designer and a portrait painter.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lABk5U0hshM/TvRmAD7_5pI/AAAAAAAAKj4/o12VrJ93S2o/s1600/16Bernini-BorgheseFlawDet.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lABk5U0hshM/TvRmAD7_5pI/AAAAAAAAKj4/o12VrJ93S2o/s320/16Bernini-BorgheseFlawDet.jpg\" width=\"209\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Bernini\u2019s father Pietro was a great sculptor too. Bernini started sculpting at the age of 8 and got noticed by the Pope Paul V.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RV2y_GfgE4I/TvRmJR929EI/AAAAAAAAKkE/I1S93ES4IA4/s1600/bernini-ecstasy-of-st-theresa-911.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RV2y_GfgE4I/TvRmJR929EI/AAAAAAAAKkE/I1S93ES4IA4/s1600/bernini-ecstasy-of-st-theresa-911.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Bernini\u2019s unique sense of light sourcing and shading, his surface textures of skin and hair far exceeded Michelangelo\u2019s.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>He molded stone like none other before him, marble into visceral, sensual sculptures. He converted hard marble to soft butter. </span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5O4ppYXGC8A/TvRiyZUZLbI/AAAAAAAAKgs/RN3Qdzw0mKI/s1600/B+rape+of+prosperina.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5O4ppYXGC8A/TvRiyZUZLbI/AAAAAAAAKgs/RN3Qdzw0mKI/s640/B+rape+of+prosperina.jpg\" width=\"497\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">He would incise the irises deeply so that they lay in shadow and appeared dark. The texture of cloth could be seen on hard marble ,the tiny wrinkles of the skin. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sBU4TbMnkoU/TvRmVV6LRDI/AAAAAAAAKkQ/vGQmF_sDfq4/s1600/C+blessed-ludovica-albertoni-.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"258\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sBU4TbMnkoU/TvRmVV6LRDI/AAAAAAAAKkQ/vGQmF_sDfq4/s320/C+blessed-ludovica-albertoni-.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Most of the time he sculpted from memory without a clay model or a subject in front of him, relying on his vision .<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Check out Bernini\u2019s David in action. He\u2019s head is turned to the left, he is obviously looking at his enemy and his face is also tense and deeply concentrated. </span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gh8VTRyscHs/TvRh9RPaqCI/AAAAAAAAKfw/7lmfmUTuczg/s1600/H+David-detail1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gh8VTRyscHs/TvRh9RPaqCI/AAAAAAAAKfw/7lmfmUTuczg/s640/H+David-detail1.jpg\" width=\"507\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">David has twisted back and is about to sling shoot Goliath. The sculpture is almost breaking out of its own pose and this provides vibrant energy to the space around it .</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oIQnrXT6L7Y/TvRiIZou1II/AAAAAAAAKf8/UTeWsUWOOy8/s1600/R+david4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">David face expression is dramatic and realistic . </span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MxL2G8cxow0/TvRiTwE4xwI/AAAAAAAAKgI/Dc462CeBTKM/s1600/T+david5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MxL2G8cxow0/TvRiTwE4xwI/AAAAAAAAKgI/Dc462CeBTKM/s640/T+david5.jpg\" width=\"450\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Bernini captured a moment \u2013a shot frozen in action. You go around the statue which is alive-- the figure is true from every angle. This is the meaning of artistic expression, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>nay--aesthetic magic. It is a real soulful 3D show.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>See the muscles sinews in the legs and how the chest is tensed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-5bLu8bbvldk/TvRmxqQh6GI/AAAAAAAAKko/24KeSnj4t3k/s1600/M++_theresa_small.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-5bLu8bbvldk/TvRmxqQh6GI/AAAAAAAAKko/24KeSnj4t3k/s320/M++_theresa_small.jpg\" width=\"222\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In comparison, Michelangelo\u2019s David statue&nbsp; <span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">below</span> is out of proportion\u2014 check out the hands and head. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I can tell you this as I am a sculptor on clay myself. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This 1:6 <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>ratio is of a ten-year-old boy. Adults have to be given 1:8.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QGzMmsCz68Q/TvRhx-Sd78I/AAAAAAAAKfk/VHmcItHIo50/s1600/David_von_Michelangelo.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">Michelangelo's David face</span><span style=\"color: red;\"> <span style=\"font-size: large;\">above</span></span> is overwrought with expression. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>And-- real HE-men do not stand in this pansy way. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>We must understand that Michelangelo was gay. </span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> The critics and the established </span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">academics have their own reputations to protect!<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-sEUR7B7O-cY/TvRm7SQ-grI/AAAAAAAAKk0/ObW6_3vNteA/s1600/Q+Martyrdom_of_St_Lawrence.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Bernini\u2019s are dramatic and active\u2014poetry in motion , literally.</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Michelangelo made his works out of a triangle, a circle, a square. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Bernini ran free \u2013 he broke out of all constricting shapes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-7tgEdOsx9G0/TvRkU-AKmNI/AAAAAAAAKiY/m79YzsHK5bA/s1600/461694856_275f1e720d_o.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-7tgEdOsx9G0/TvRkU-AKmNI/AAAAAAAAKiY/m79YzsHK5bA/s320/461694856_275f1e720d_o.jpg\" width=\"212\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; It is totally out of proportion with respect to age. Mary looks like a young female with a man\u2019s face. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Jesus was thirty three when he died and his lifeless body cannot be so reed like and slender.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; 16 November 1923 in Murom - 22\nOctober 2002) , whose books are the prescribed practice material for\nnational and International Physics Olympiads.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Igor Irodov was born in\nMurom, Vladimir Oblast, RSFSR. In 1931 his family moved to Moscow. Igor Irodov\nserved in the Soviet Army during the World War II between 16 October 1941 and\n23 November 1945. &nbsp;In 1946 he was admitted to Moscow Engineering Physics\nInstitute. &nbsp;Igor Irodov received his Kandidat of Physical and Mathematical\nSciences degree from Moscow Engineering Physics Institute in 1954.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Igor Irodov was a faculty member of the Moscow Engineering\nPhysics Institute since that time until his death. Since 1977 he was a\nProfessor of the \"General Physics\" chair. &nbsp;He spent 27 years of his\nlife creating a full course of General Physics.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: normal; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FjOpudvb7o0/UHqvFOJGnkI/AAAAAAAAVHk/lTJ6pKNuRzE/s1600/2jui8oikgm.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FjOpudvb7o0/UHqvFOJGnkI/AAAAAAAAVHk/lTJ6pKNuRzE/s400/2jui8oikgm.gif\" height=\"266\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large;\">Above : A genius who graced planet earth , who made a real dent in this universe - &nbsp;who died UNSUNG ! We , the world citizens&nbsp;honor&nbsp;you! &nbsp;RIP, sir !</span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; After reading them you will still be in fog.&nbsp; This post contains the essence in a couple of pages-- and you will finally be transported from darkness to light.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">WHAT FOLLOWS IS WHY STEVE JOBS CAME TO INDIA, AS A YOUNG MAN-- WHY THOUSANDS OF HIPPIES CAME TO INDIA IN THE SIXTIES , SOUGHT THE TRUTH -- AND WENT BACK TO FORM THE INTERNET -- TO CUT THE STRENGTH OF BIG BROTHER</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This lucid explantion is for people of this planet who still wonder what the fuss of Vedas and Upanishads are all about. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HxzsxOXVYcU/TvA-Na8pRgI/AAAAAAAAKbg/yuckzyW0_3I/s1600/383px-Sun_temple_martand_indogreek.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"282\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HxzsxOXVYcU/TvA-Na8pRgI/AAAAAAAAKbg/yuckzyW0_3I/s400/383px-Sun_temple_martand_indogreek.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hXwhz7TfSA4/TurQnuMpFMI/AAAAAAAAJ64/fNM4jXJQ040/s1600/imagesCAM92TRI.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hXwhz7TfSA4/TurQnuMpFMI/AAAAAAAAJ64/fNM4jXJQ040/s1600/imagesCAM92TRI.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedas and the Upanishads are to India what the Crown and Scepter are to an anointed king. They are India's proudest and most ancient possessions. It hardly matters if you are a Christian or a Muslim or even a Pakistani-as long as you have Indian DNA. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>For Vedas are NOT about religion.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xi6nxI0gMmo/TurdpPSb9FI/AAAAAAAAKCg/t04T34Gw5gw/s1600/imagesCAN797A0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xi6nxI0gMmo/TurdpPSb9FI/AAAAAAAAKCg/t04T34Gw5gw/s1600/imagesCAN797A0.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In India the low castes have often expressed that Vedas have given them a raw deal. This is NOT true. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Vedic Sanatana Dharma system has the 4 classes, or graded inequality to sustain society.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yDsZ4daQVIg/TurQ-t4-mhI/AAAAAAAAJ7I/kbVYhXtqHj8/s1600/wer.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yDsZ4daQVIg/TurQ-t4-mhI/AAAAAAAAJ7I/kbVYhXtqHj8/s1600/wer.png\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Brahmins, Kshatriyas, Vaishyas and Shudras. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This is like a ship\u2019s crew list, where everybody has a job to do, to maintain team harmonics. There has to be Navigators and there has to be Engineers or the ship will have a breakdown. Or in a Cricket team everybody cannot be batsmen, somebody has to bowl.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-sQQ6negMj7k/TurQSfHmccI/AAAAAAAAJ6o/PYN23uOaDbA/s1600/www.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-sQQ6negMj7k/TurQSfHmccI/AAAAAAAAJ6o/PYN23uOaDbA/s1600/www.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">From 9000 BC to 5000 BC Vedas were transmitted orally by learning vast amounts of verses by heart. There is no more time available after a period of rest to do daily chores. The Kshatriya warriors had to stay in camps , rigorously practice their backsides off , and fight, they too could not be expected to do usual chores. Which left out the Vaishyas and the Shudras , who distributed the remaining among themselves. Those days we just produced food, as there were no industries. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Vaishyas handled even medicine and surgery.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mgpUJ4aZm8w/TurS_drSDzI/AAAAAAAAJ9g/2b9jotCwUwY/s1600/imagesCAPUMOQA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mgpUJ4aZm8w/TurS_drSDzI/AAAAAAAAJ9g/2b9jotCwUwY/s1600/imagesCAPUMOQA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">The original Vedas do NOT contain texts where it is said that Brahmins were created out of the head , Khsatriyas out of the arms , Vaishyas out of the thighs and Shudras were created out of the feet.</span> </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">The word Brahm<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">A</span>n denoted the Supreme God, and NOT Brahm<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">I</span>n the high caste human being.</span> </span><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">watch the video below , to understand brahm<span style=\"background-color: lime;\">A</span>n.</span> </em>  <br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em>It is a&nbsp; passage from \"BrihadAranyaka\" (major forest) Upanishad. An interlocution between sage Yajnyavalkya and Shakalya regarding number of Gods. When sage Yajnyavalkya was presented with thousand cows by King Janaka of Videha, other Brahmins became jealous, and one by one started questioning Yajnyavalkya. Then it was Vidagdha Sakalya's turn who queried Yajnyavalkya regarding number of Gods.<o:p></o:p></em></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/f13w7NCqmyc/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/f13w7NCqmyc&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/f13w7NCqmyc&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The caste systems were polarised by foreign invaders who wanted to divide and rule ( very easy when you have infighting in the family ) &nbsp;\u2014 and they were indeed very successful. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\">The ancient Maharishis were peaceful and graceful souls and incapable of being racists.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yPuidus3aS4/TurTP2YuCmI/AAAAAAAAJ9w/oh7WPBR6eNk/s1600/imagesCAVIUHOJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yPuidus3aS4/TurTP2YuCmI/AAAAAAAAJ9w/oh7WPBR6eNk/s1600/imagesCAVIUHOJ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If all want to be architects a skyscraper cannot be built. We need masons, carpenters, people who are not afraid of heights etc\u2014it is a team contribution. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>From 9000 BC to 5000 BC, the<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Vedas were learnt by heart and transmitted orally from teacher to pupil, belonging to the Brahmin class.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fkQrUDEYsO4/TurdwFJiQZI/AAAAAAAAKCo/wKuTqwBEJfo/s1600/imagesCA8OFUQC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fkQrUDEYsO4/TurdwFJiQZI/AAAAAAAAKCo/wKuTqwBEJfo/s1600/imagesCA8OFUQC.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In Kerala the shrewd Namboodiri Brahmins hijacked the caste system, and forced the Vaishya and Shudra women to expose their breasts in public. They would NOT allow&nbsp;a Kshatriya&nbsp; ( their pet Rottweilers warriors ) to come within 6 feet, Vaishya to come within 32 feet and a Shudra to come withing  72 feet of them. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">All this is NOT written in the original Vedas</span>.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">All this is as criminal as the MD of a company criminally changing the Company\u2019s rule book , so that he can molest all the females and sodomise all the men , working in the office, officially .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mMYwQVtTuaU/TurTGp7R0rI/AAAAAAAAJ9o/ROu6aZl8TLo/s1600/imagesCADQLM9H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mMYwQVtTuaU/TurTGp7R0rI/AAAAAAAAJ9o/ROu6aZl8TLo/s1600/imagesCADQLM9H.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedas are considered the earliest literary record of this planet and were written on the banks of the river Saraswati. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The Saraswati civilization was the oldest in the world and flourished on the banks of the river Saraswati from 9000 BC to 4000 BC, till the river became non-perennial, due to a tectonic shift blocking the river\u2019s mouth at the Himalayan Glacier. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The 4 Vedas along with the 108 Upanishads are the most sacred books of India.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0IqmE1f3_4M/Turd4ds9FhI/AAAAAAAAKCw/V1COo3AfipI/s1600/imagesCA47TVFY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0IqmE1f3_4M/Turd4ds9FhI/AAAAAAAAKCw/V1COo3AfipI/s320/imagesCA47TVFY.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Without knowing the Vedas one cannot comprehend the inner soul and heights of Indian glory.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> A brilliant man like Schopenhauer found the Upanishads to be the \"solace\" of his life and death, and Kant found the Hindus were \"gentle\", that \"all nations are tolerated amongst them.\" . India has the unique record of never attacking any country in the past history. These ancient texts won the admiration of eminent human beings of the caliber of Carl Jung, Emerson, Thoreau, Walt Whitman, Victor Hugo, Romain Rolland, Hermann Hesse, Henrich Zimmer, Tolstoy, Sir Edwin Arnold, Yeats, Toynbee and hundreds of others.</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-HRFqeUSUxrA/TurTW48HOCI/AAAAAAAAJ94/b9Wlgt5F2Vo/s1600/imagesCA857FK4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-HRFqeUSUxrA/TurTW48HOCI/AAAAAAAAJ94/b9Wlgt5F2Vo/s1600/imagesCA857FK4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedas <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>hold the original scriptures of <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Sanatana Dharma ( Hindu ) <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>teachings, and contain spiritual knowledge encompassing every possible aspects of Indian life. Vedic literature with its philosophical maxims has stood the test of nearly 11000 years of time <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and is the highest religious authority for the Hindu in particular and probably for the whole of mankind in future. The world is waking up to a few books written 7000 years ago.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-P_SRBX0B0lU/TurTdse8XzI/AAAAAAAAJ-A/TsMK3MFp8uc/s1600/imagesCADQLM9H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-P_SRBX0B0lU/TurTdse8XzI/AAAAAAAAJ-A/TsMK3MFp8uc/s1600/imagesCADQLM9H.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On Dec 21<sup>st</sup> 2012, man must upgrade his DNA to achieve 12 strand nil junk from 2 strand, 96% junk . There is only one source of wisdom to achieve this , the timeless Vedas and the Upanishads. These are not shepherds\u2019 verses as ridiculed by jealous Vatican- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>but an amazing encyclopedia of the most mind boggling philosophy of thought. It must be remembered that 7000 years ago, the whole world outside India were eating raw meat, living in caves and going grunt grunt for language.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6g6-Vg6PXeo/Turd9iXCUzI/AAAAAAAAKC4/URVQ7hL4laM/s1600/imagesCAN3HB84.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6g6-Vg6PXeo/Turd9iXCUzI/AAAAAAAAKC4/URVQ7hL4laM/s1600/imagesCAN3HB84.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u201cVeda\u201d means wisdom, and it manifests the language of the gods in Sanskrit. The laws of the Vedas in amazing Sanskrit verses , regulate the bedrock of culture and customs of the Hindus to this present day. Hindu religion is run by the laws of Dharma. All the obligatory duties of the Hindu owe their allegiance to the Vedas.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>They draw forth the thought of successive generations of Maharshi seers<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>or spiritual giants from 9500 BC to 5000 BC.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tUs1hvcxjn0/TurTjtoRIeI/AAAAAAAAJ-I/kTg7rHCb92E/s1600/imagesCAX6RAD9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"145\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tUs1hvcxjn0/TurTjtoRIeI/AAAAAAAAJ-I/kTg7rHCb92E/s320/imagesCAX6RAD9.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedas are four: The Rig-Veda, the Sama Veda, the Yajur Veda and the Atharva Veda, the Rig Veda written in 5000 BC being the main.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"background-color: white; line-height: 150%;\">Each Veda consists of four parts \u2013 the Samhitas (hymns), the Brahmanas (rituals), the Aranyakas (theologies) and the Upanishads (philosophies). The Upanishads form the concluding portions of the Veda and therefore called the \u201cVedanta\u201d or the end of the Veda and contains the essence of Vedic teachings.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jpiqiaXeyRY/TureEymYSkI/AAAAAAAAKDA/T6cuKMaZKX0/s1600/imagesCAEVZA5D.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jpiqiaXeyRY/TureEymYSkI/AAAAAAAAKDA/T6cuKMaZKX0/s1600/imagesCAEVZA5D.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedas in its unchanged unabridged format in Sanskrit verses , have guided the Indian\u2019s<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>religious direction for ages and will continue to do so till our sun goes supernova. The Rig-Veda is a \u2018samhita\u2019 or collection of mantras consists of 1,017 hymns ( \u2018suktas\u2019 ), covering about 10,600 stanzas, divided into eight \u2018astakas\u2019 each having eight \u2018adhayayas\u2019 ( chapters ), which are again sub-divided into various groups. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vqeiEzq9MAU/TurTposBXvI/AAAAAAAAJ-Q/Pl6wrwwuo4U/s1600/imagesCAVLGFNS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vqeiEzq9MAU/TurTposBXvI/AAAAAAAAJ-Q/Pl6wrwwuo4U/s1600/imagesCAVLGFNS.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The seven primary Maharshi seers ( Sapta Rishis )<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>involved with the oral composition of the Vedas by divine channeling are rishis : Atri, Kanwa,Vashistha, Vishwamitra, Jamadagni, Gotama and Bharadwaja. This was an era of unbridled non-individuality. Knowledge was not patented , like what it is done now by narrow minds. It is such a disgrace that people like Isaac Newton ( Calculus ) , Nobel prize winner Herman Hesse ( philosophy ) and dozens of others became heroes of the current era by patenting stolen Vedic knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LrpAW7D5af4/TurRPuycCeI/AAAAAAAAJ7g/NHUbTmdoapM/s1600/download+%25281%2529.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LrpAW7D5af4/TurRPuycCeI/AAAAAAAAJ7g/NHUbTmdoapM/s1600/download+%25281%2529.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The whole of the West tried even to prove that Aryan invasion happened inwards, so that they could claim credit for writing the Vedas. In this DNA age, all these fraudulent claims have been consigned to the dustbin of history.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-N_LNSpJuFF0/TurePObMJfI/AAAAAAAAKDQ/zuwfiNLfS_8/s1600/imagesCASK1J2E.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-N_LNSpJuFF0/TurePObMJfI/AAAAAAAAKDQ/zuwfiNLfS_8/s1600/imagesCASK1J2E.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">These Vedic texts include hymns, liturgical instructions, and philosophical courses . The ancient Maharishi 11000 years ago , were </span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Epistemologists</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> whose theories deal with puzzles about the source, nature, foundation, scope, validity and limits of human knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bFwvIJGlJPQ/TureKQz_QBI/AAAAAAAAKDI/iBGK8GIVbuQ/s1600/imagesCASMOIWL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bFwvIJGlJPQ/TureKQz_QBI/AAAAAAAAKDI/iBGK8GIVbuQ/s1600/imagesCASMOIWL.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vedas show how ancient rishis experienced the divine reality and how they responded with exuberant joy, confidence and a feeling of intimacy. This literature is not rustic or primitive but highly developed in its literary form, in its intellectual insight, and in its questioning attitude. The glory of this vast literature is its imaginative and emotional qualities.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NxiAn9Zlbbg/TurRMC_50CI/AAAAAAAAJ7Y/MO0PDg-_hcI/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NxiAn9Zlbbg/TurRMC_50CI/AAAAAAAAJ7Y/MO0PDg-_hcI/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Maharishis were experts in Metaphysics<b> </b></span></span><span class=\"artcopy\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">to determine the real nature of things\u2014to determine the meaning, structure, and principles of whatever is in so far as it is-- with reality as a whole.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> It is a call to recognize the existence and overwhelming importance of a set of higher realities that ordinary men could not deduce--the science of ultimate reality , as opposed to appearance or the contrast between appearance and reality . A cloud appears to consist of some white, fleecy substance, although in reality it is a concentration of drops of water. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FQljQ_u_O58/TurRI2AO9yI/AAAAAAAAJ7Q/Pcg2BCIs0Xo/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FQljQ_u_O58/TurRI2AO9yI/AAAAAAAAJ7Q/Pcg2BCIs0Xo/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is the<b> </b>study and science of first principles or ultimate irrefutable truths. The two descriptions of the subject would thus be two sides of a single coin. Scientific theories can be brought to the test of experience, whereas metaphysical theories cannot. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The Vedic metaphysician was a sort of super scientist, unlimited in his curiosity and gifted with a capacity for putting together other people's findings with a skill and imagination that none of them individually commands. He can refute by debate, through a method for systematic evaluation of definitions<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Jd8VK8Rj7RM/TureVKgMuWI/AAAAAAAAKDY/a3Y4fsu1Bro/s1600/imagesCAVKA3N6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Jd8VK8Rj7RM/TureVKgMuWI/AAAAAAAAKDY/a3Y4fsu1Bro/s1600/imagesCAVKA3N6.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"inlinetitle\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Indian rishis were the first to engage their great minds in dialectics</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> in philosophy\u2014the<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>method of investigating the nature of truth by the criticism of initial concepts and hypotheses\u2014all in the most peaceful natural surroundings <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>.The ancient Indian Vedic d<span class=\"inlinetitle\">ialectic is based on a dialogue between two or more rishis , master or student - people who may hold differing views, yet wish to pursue truth by seeking agreement with one another.&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\"></span><span class=\"inlinetitle\">This is in contrast to debate, in which two or more people hold differing views and wish to persuade or prove one another wrong (and thus a jury or judge is needed to decide the matter), or rhetoric, which is a relatively long monologue oration conducted by a single stupid person.</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedas are not puerile babblings of rustic troubadours or minstrels , but sedate out-pourings of exceptionally sharp and graceful minds in quest of truth . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Like indestructible diamonds of brilliant fire they have come down 11000 years in spotless perfection, with no need to be revised or abridged, to suit the modern era. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IrWuKrwYFjY/TurSUDwAo-I/AAAAAAAAJ8w/zfnf5Sqebp0/s1600/A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IrWuKrwYFjY/TurSUDwAo-I/AAAAAAAAJ8w/zfnf5Sqebp0/s1600/A.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">From the Vedas evolved the Upanishads, whose copious enquiries into the nature of man, the Universe, and God, strike the intelligent and high IQ modern scientific mind with speechless wonder. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Vedas are verses written in <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">the most digitally perfect language in the world, Sanskrit, with a scientific alphabet and perfected vocabulary, and a grammar which is itself a great work of art.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Vedic seers , propounded six systems of philosophy explaining man, universe, and God, before which Aristotle's and Plato's theories look like juvenile endeavors. They discovered the Earth's rotatory and revolutionary motions, and studied the courses of constellations and stars, and founded the twin sciences of astronomy and astrology. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CrOZlgc-oik/TureeFx88nI/AAAAAAAAKDg/6vJpp8YbOOg/s1600/imagesCAOEJYSB.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CrOZlgc-oik/TureeFx88nI/AAAAAAAAKDg/6vJpp8YbOOg/s1600/imagesCAOEJYSB.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThey probed the human anatomy , and perfected a system of medicine for the holistic welfare of the body, evolved the science of Yoga for the health of the mind, and the Tantra Shastra to develop the psychic and esoteric forces latent in man's being. They brought out Dharma Sastras to guide man's conduct in society, Grihya Sutras to guide the conduct of house-holders, and a unique science, Meemamsa, prescribing bloodless sacrificial lore for the attainment of individual and national prosperity. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--B6m8HQfpgM/TurejkZENZI/AAAAAAAAKDo/M91VHVFI3cY/s1600/imagesCAQB4KY7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"152\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/--B6m8HQfpgM/TurejkZENZI/AAAAAAAAKDo/M91VHVFI3cY/s320/imagesCAQB4KY7.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThey codified the laws of sanitation, town-planning, architecture, sculpture and enunciated the principles of classical music, dancing, and the art of love. They laid down principles of state-craft, and of the art of war, with human and animal strategy, with physical weapons, or shastras, and enchanted weapons or astras.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uC9IOhemTZo/TurSIg7jpfI/AAAAAAAAJ8g/v-lhV9SCjak/s1600/imagesCAMM3BW3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uC9IOhemTZo/TurSIg7jpfI/AAAAAAAAJ8g/v-lhV9SCjak/s1600/imagesCAMM3BW3.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">For example here is the Vedic set of rules for war termed Dharma Yuddha -<span style=\"color: #333333;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Fighting must begin no earlier than sunrise and end exactly at sunset.</span><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 5pt; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Multiple warriors may not attack a single warrior.</span><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 5pt; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Two warriors may \u201cduel\u201d, or engage in prolonged personal combat, only if they carry the same weapons and they are on the same mount (no mount, a horse, an elephant, or a chariot).</span><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 5pt; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>No warrior may kill or injure a warrior who has surrendered.</span><span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 5pt; tab-stops: list .5in; text-indent: -0.25in;\">\n<span style=\"color: #090909; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>One who surrenders becomes a prisoner of war and will then be subject to the protections of a prisoner of war.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>No warrior may kill or injure an unarmed warrior.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>No warrior may kill or injure a person or animal not taking part in the war.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: black;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; Vedas introduced Consciousness , the most valuable thing on this planet , to Western philosophical thought. The Vedas are considered to be eternal, without beginning and end as they represent the divine truth itself as perceived through the elevated consciousness of great seers. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bDbJLSzeyQE/TurfLlPh-HI/AAAAAAAAKEY/mA2qj2YJjzs/s1600/images%252B%25252870%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bDbJLSzeyQE/TurfLlPh-HI/AAAAAAAAKEY/mA2qj2YJjzs/s1600/images%252B%25252870%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nVedas teach us that creation is without beginning or end. Science has proved to us that the sum total of cosmic energy is always the same. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The ancient Vedic rishis in all their wisdom said as early as 9000 BC , that our universe is not woven from<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>matter but consciousness. These seers and channels said,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>that the universal laws are clear, your attitude about your life will shape it , that Matter, energy and consciousness are interchangeable. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Cm2K3ritCFA/TurfRWoocBI/AAAAAAAAKEg/_YqDsrOZQxA/s1600/128_19_04_09_6_49_52.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Cm2K3ritCFA/TurfRWoocBI/AAAAAAAAKEg/_YqDsrOZQxA/s320/128_19_04_09_6_49_52.jpg\" width=\"229\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nConsciousness is the intelligence, the organising principle behind the arising of form, unlike what Darwin says . There is a consciousness in every molecule of matter. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>All atoms in the entire universe are capable of mind reading and communicating with other atoms. The expanded abilities of self awareness is abstract reasoning, free will, creativity, foresight etc.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-4bazncA35Zw/TurR1t0AS9I/AAAAAAAAJ8I/QpeT4V7BKco/s1600/rr.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-4bazncA35Zw/TurR1t0AS9I/AAAAAAAAJ8I/QpeT4V7BKco/s1600/rr.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nOur modern culture is oriented towards reducing one\u2019s self awareness rather than expanding it. After the ancient Vedic rishis, it is the flower children ( hippies ) of the sixties , who took on big brother and tried to expand it. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>On the subatomic level\u2014mind is over matter. The brain and DNA is governed by the laws of quantum physics rather than the laws of biology or neurophysiology. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Scalar waves ( made famous by Nikola Tesla ) is the point of fundamental intersection where matter and consciousness<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>influence each other<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nVedic scriptures may be classified into two divisions: <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Sruti </span>scriptures and <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Smriti</span> scriptures. <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Sruti</span> in Sanskrit means \"that which is heard.\" . Sruti include the Vedas (Rig, Yajur, Sama and Atharva) and the Bhagavad Gita<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThus the Vedas are the eternal truths that the Vedic seers, called rishis, are said to have heard during their deep meditations. The Vedas are not considered the works of the human mind, but an expression of what has been realized through intuitive perception by Vedic rishis, who had powers to see beyond the physical phenomena. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>At a later date, after 4000 years of oral transmission from master to pupil, in 5000 BC , these were compiled by Sage Vyasa for the benefit of future generations. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nTo the Hindu, Shruti is what cannot be thought up by the limited human intellect, but is of divine origin.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>It is what is forever valid, never changes, is not dependent on the limited capacity for understanding of any one historical person or human founder . The Hindu for this reason is proud not to need a historical founder. The founder and foundation of the Vedas and the Upanishads is the Supreme<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>force itself, is what is indestructible and timeless.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-X_nto4U7uOw/TurRvk8caQI/AAAAAAAAJ8A/eiPFYXDdMF0/s1600/untitledvvbn.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-X_nto4U7uOw/TurRvk8caQI/AAAAAAAAJ8A/eiPFYXDdMF0/s1600/untitledvvbn.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vedic revelations are so cosmic that they approach more closely the findings of modern quantum physics and astronomy than the pious pronouncements of rabid preachers. The rishis made claims so cosmic that even modern physics seems only to be catching up with them and realizing, after every scientific breakthrough, that the ancients were there long before them.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Smriti means \"that which is remembered.\" Smriti scriptures are derived from the Vedas and are considered to be of human origin and not of divine origin. They were written to explain and elaborate the Vedas, making them understandable and more meaningful to the general population. All authoritative writings outside the Vedas are collectively referred to as Smriti. Smriti include the Dharma Shastras, Nibhandas, Puranas, The Epics, Agamas or Tantras, Darshanas and Vedangas (Upa Vedas).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Vedas<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>are the world's oldest intellectual legacies. They are the only composition in the universe invested with Divine origin, and hence divine sanctity. They have been heirlooms of the Hindus from generation to generation for the past 11000 years. The Vedas are the discoveries of the laws of nature, the world and the beings living in it and the Ultimate Truth. They are called <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">apauruseya grantha</span> (authorless works) .<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Vedas record the spiritual experiences of souls strongly endowed with the sense for reality. </span>They are held to be authoritative on the ground that they express the experiences of the experts in the field of religion. The Vedas bring together different ways in which the religious-minded of that era experienced reality and describe the general principles of religious knowledge and growth. The experiences themselves are of a varied character, so their records are many-sided (visvatomukham) or 'suggestive of many interpretations' (anekarthatam).<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Vedas are the quintessence of classical Hindu philosophy. Thinking with your heart; loving with your mind. All yoga and meditation aim to attain this goal. Anything else is Maya delusion, or worse. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>And when the heart sees, it sees the unknowable, nameless, formless, limitless, supreme God. He is called the nonexistent because he is eternal, beyond existence. God manifest is the fabric of creation itself. They are one.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>They explain the nature of the universe, of life, while admitting that Creation itself is the one unknowable mystery. </div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nTo the Vedic sages, creation indicated that point before which there was no Creator, the line between indefinable nothingness and something delineated by attributes and function, at least. Like the moment before the Big Bang Theory. These concepts preoccupy high wisdom, the Truth far removed from mere religion. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Vedas are the inspired utterances of a whole galaxy of realized souls, of spiritual geniuses, of people not merely well versed intellectually but with spiritual enlightenment.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Vedic hymns are used today at Hindu wedding ceremonies, and temple and school prayers <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>in an astonishing example of continuous tradition. The feat of memorizing and handing down a vast amount of oral literature is a hallmark of Hinduism.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-PjxJGJerceo/Tura0mlkVhI/AAAAAAAAKCQ/ZcDg3qHQOzM/s1600/imagesCACSSCW8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Vedas and Upanishads thus work in a Tamas Rajas ( Yin Yang ) way.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nIts most famous formulation is one of the mahavakyas or \u201cgreat formulae\u201d: <o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">Tat tvam asi, \u201cYou are That\u201d.</span> </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4J68VL9Edj8/TusivONt1xI/AAAAAAAAKFI/RcTPpD91skU/s1600/imagesBBN.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4J68VL9Edj8/TusivONt1xI/AAAAAAAAKFI/RcTPpD91skU/s1600/imagesBBN.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">The Chandogya Upanishad--</b> <i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">What does it mean? It means that you are none other than God. Who else is God, if not you?</i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-e1fXuc1QiqA/TusizkpVqdI/AAAAAAAAKFQ/vHTIL95X6TI/s1600/imagesCARFZ5US.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-e1fXuc1QiqA/TusizkpVqdI/AAAAAAAAKFQ/vHTIL95X6TI/s1600/imagesCARFZ5US.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rXY-hYc0i24/Tusi4Ic2wjI/AAAAAAAAKFY/8XDx5mlBKO8/s1600/tumblr_ligu28WzgB1qzw12oo1_500.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"238\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rXY-hYc0i24/Tusi4Ic2wjI/AAAAAAAAKFY/8XDx5mlBKO8/s320/tumblr_ligu28WzgB1qzw12oo1_500.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4RvqOEQOcy4/TurVV4t_sjI/AAAAAAAAKAA/0h99-tAirBI/s1600/imagesCA81XOXU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4RvqOEQOcy4/TurVV4t_sjI/AAAAAAAAKAA/0h99-tAirBI/s1600/imagesCA81XOXU.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nVedanta taught the technique of self-development. The ultimate destiny of man is to discover within himself the true Self as the changeless behind the changing, the eternal behind the ephemeral, and the infinite behind the finite. Greater wisdom was never compressed into three little words than by the Chandogya Upanishad which proclaimed the true Self of man as part of the Infinite Spirit - tat twam asi: \"That Thou Art\".<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
