follows-- to get the feel.</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nUpanishads are the divine revelations received by ancient seers. The sages who gave them to us did not care to leave their names; the truths they set down were eternal, and the identity of those who arranged the words irrelevant.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-feOTjfShZkY/Tural0Ip94I/AAAAAAAAKCA/VdvNi-qLNAc/s1600/imagesCA3YAG4X.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-feOTjfShZkY/Tural0Ip94I/AAAAAAAAKCA/VdvNi-qLNAc/s1600/imagesCA3YAG4X.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">They represent the essence of the Vedas, the greatest truths ever known to mankind. The Upanishads are humanity's most profound philosophical inquiry and the first perceptions of the unity of all, the oneness of man and God. </span>The Upanishads are also called the Vedanta. </div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe literal meaning of Vedanta is 'the end of the Vedas.' <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>They were written down around 5000 BC, but conveyed by word of mouth from 9000 BC to 4000 BC. The basic teaching of the Upanishads is that the essence of all beings - from a leaf to the perfect human being - and all things is the Divine Spirit, called Brahman. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eWfmBdUVuBo/TurVGp7Pw1I/AAAAAAAAJ_4/wQjOY_8UFvI/s1600/imagesCAIPO1M2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eWfmBdUVuBo/TurVGp7Pw1I/AAAAAAAAJ_4/wQjOY_8UFvI/s1600/imagesCAIPO1M2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Vatican has long tried to ridicule Hinduism by giving propaganda that a Shiva lingam is a penis set inside a vagina. A shiva lingam is a meteoric black stone and it represents Shiva\u2019s Pineal Gland. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Our amazing Tantras were reduced to sex orgies. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-UAeAAD4sgWs/TuragDqR5KI/AAAAAAAAKB4/9ZZliro9czc/s1600/imagesCAMIIVA2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-UAeAAD4sgWs/TuragDqR5KI/AAAAAAAAKB4/9ZZliro9czc/s1600/imagesCAMIIVA2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">You cannot be a Hindu heretic , or get people burnt on the stake , because there is no standard set of dogmas in Hindu faith , written or unwritten, from which deviation could make you a heretic.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Openness is the essence of Hinduism. Gratitude is inherent, which makes this religion noble . Example: A Hindu will never ever neglect his aged and vulnerable parents. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ET7HHsWI2ro/TuraaqaltBI/AAAAAAAAKBw/NXR6A8wcGg4/s1600/imagesCARGS5L4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ET7HHsWI2ro/TuraaqaltBI/AAAAAAAAKBw/NXR6A8wcGg4/s1600/imagesCARGS5L4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Divorce rate within Hindus is the lowest in the world--it is a mindset . Marriage is NOT based on lust, but by sacred commitment of 7 pheras<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>around a holy fire.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A true Hindu will not exploit vulnerability. Hinduism does not allow you to breach a trust. When a Hindu says \"thank you\", he really means it. When a Hindu greets you with a Namaste, he bows to the greatness in you. There is great tolerance to other cultures and spiritual paths. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-dCooFlzhuHA/TurVkA_kwJI/AAAAAAAAKAI/iAqk1yfZFTo/s1600/imagesCA2RGXPH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-dCooFlzhuHA/TurVkA_kwJI/AAAAAAAAKAI/iAqk1yfZFTo/s1600/imagesCA2RGXPH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The heart of Hinduism is oneness and inclusivity.. The Vedic rishis had stressed, there are many paths to the final goal. This is why Hinduism has a multiplicity of Gods and Goddesses. This is why Hinduism abjures all divides and separates. It happily embraces all different paths. Hinduism is a spiritual code. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Know thyself is the quintessence. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It has no founder or a Supreme head.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NaTDtsqkzW0/TurVwWO5U-I/AAAAAAAAKAQ/MNTfLcFnR5o/s1600/imagesCA4D7J01.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NaTDtsqkzW0/TurVwWO5U-I/AAAAAAAAKAQ/MNTfLcFnR5o/s1600/imagesCA4D7J01.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>There is NO supreme middleman like the Pope who can canonise a human into a saint, by giving bullshit, to the unsuspecting masses. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It is a movement based on principles or evolved over time code of<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Dharma. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It is a relentless pursuit of truth, flexible to suit all situations. Hinduism does NOT care for individual leadership or hierarchy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VZTp_9f7FKw/TurU-dHIBpI/AAAAAAAAJ_w/nBMwFLA9aV4/s1600/imagesCA8UFBID.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VZTp_9f7FKw/TurU-dHIBpI/AAAAAAAAJ_w/nBMwFLA9aV4/s1600/imagesCA8UFBID.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nFree from theology and dogma, the Upanishads remain the primary source of inspiration and guidance for millions of Hindus and non-Hindus alike. <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">They have influenced many Western thinkers, including von Gothe, Arthur Schopenhauer, Ralph Waldo Emerson. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4--UB9IzNvQ/TuraTlTDmyI/AAAAAAAAKBo/pG1u2S3RsZM/s1600/imagesCASF77CP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4--UB9IzNvQ/TuraTlTDmyI/AAAAAAAAKBo/pG1u2S3RsZM/s1600/imagesCASF77CP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">The Upanishads are the concluding portions of the Vedas and the teachings based on them is called Vedanta.</span> The Upanishads focus on philosophical questions such as the purpose of life, origin of the universe, concepts of time, space and matter, as well as concepts of atman, Brahman, maya, immortality, rebirth, karma, and the world. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UiMU3vtcFoM/TurWESPjxGI/AAAAAAAAKAY/pufkjcN9QEM/s1600/imagesCA84N6AH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UiMU3vtcFoM/TurWESPjxGI/AAAAAAAAKAY/pufkjcN9QEM/s1600/imagesCA84N6AH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nAccording to our Indian tradition, there were once 1,180 Upanishads. Of the 108 Upanishads that have been preserved, the following thirteen are generally considered to be the principal Upanishads: The Isa, Katha, Kena, Prasna, Mundaka, Mandhukya, Chandogya, Brhadaranyaka, Taittiriya, Aitareya, Svetasvatara, Kaivalya and Maitri. </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zXAG2OqkwDA/TurWJ1o6NnI/AAAAAAAAKAg/yJ-ZFuSmR1Y/s1600/imagesCAFSZOUA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zXAG2OqkwDA/TurWJ1o6NnI/AAAAAAAAKAg/yJ-ZFuSmR1Y/s1600/imagesCAFSZOUA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Upanishads are known as the Vedanta, both because chronologically they come at the end of the Vedas and also because philosophically they represent the noblest upshot, the highest watermark of the Vedic civilization and genius. One meaning of the word Upanishad is to sit nearby. In the Indian tradition, the guru would be seated under a tree, near a river or lake, and one or more disciples would cluster around him to learnt he wisdom. They are the dialogues between guru and sisya\u2014the teacher and student. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6mOKW7mmbzE/TurWm_3nNRI/AAAAAAAAKAo/6VK4NmDSBSU/s1600/imagesCAC3RZAX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6mOKW7mmbzE/TurWm_3nNRI/AAAAAAAAKAo/6VK4NmDSBSU/s1600/imagesCAC3RZAX.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Upanishads are the remarkable compositions, which contain sublime and philosophical speculations concerning the Universal Soul, and cosmic consciousness. The Upanishads declare that Karmas give us only perishable fruits and that jnana (knowledge) alone can lead to immortality. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6wv3d4UoEK8/TurWsVYVNpI/AAAAAAAAKAw/Ymwrf8GutAA/s1600/imagesCAOG7T53.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6wv3d4UoEK8/TurWsVYVNpI/AAAAAAAAKAw/Ymwrf8GutAA/s1600/imagesCAOG7T53.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Upanishads tell us that there is a Reality underlying life which rituals cannot reach, next to which the things we see and touch in everyday life are shadows. They teach that this Reality is the essence of every created thing, and the same Reality is our real Self so that each of us is one with the power that created and sustains the universe. The Upanishads are not philosophy but are darshanas, \u201csomething seen\u201d and therefore to be realized. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-zp6klP-WdG8/TurU3IaPl3I/AAAAAAAAJ_o/DlpibhCKZjM/s1600/images%252B%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-zp6klP-WdG8/TurU3IaPl3I/AAAAAAAAJ_o/DlpibhCKZjM/s1600/images%252B%252812%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n\"As flowing rivers disappear into the sea, losing their name and form, thus a wise man, freed from name and form, goes to the divine person who is beyond all.\" - <b>Mundaka Upanishad</b> iii 2. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3mfl6HtO8-0/TuraLytNhcI/AAAAAAAAKBg/ZcH6SYJWhKk/s1600/imagesCAUERPRD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3mfl6HtO8-0/TuraLytNhcI/AAAAAAAAKBg/ZcH6SYJWhKk/s1600/imagesCAUERPRD.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">The Upanishads are crammed with thoughts that wander through eternity.</span> Their message is that there is far more to life than success, and far more to success than money; and there can be no higher destiny for man than to be engaged in endless seeking after endless truth. They give <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>answers to the three<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>questions :<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">\"Where is the life we have lost in living\"<br />\nWhere is the wisdom we have lost in knowledge?<br />\nWhere is the knowledge we have lost in information?</i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-34dK70ToolM/TuraGUMJ1yI/AAAAAAAAKBY/1MTowBSYfs8/s1600/imagesCAXT1HBL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-34dK70ToolM/TuraGUMJ1yI/AAAAAAAAKBY/1MTowBSYfs8/s1600/imagesCAXT1HBL.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Rishis had repeatedly emphasized that the ultimate reality lies beyond the realms of the senses and the grey matter beneath our skulls. Hark again to the Upanishads:<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">\"There the eye goes not<o:p></o:p></i><br />\n<br />\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">Speech goes not, nor the mind.<o:p></o:p></i><br />\n<br />\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">We know not, we understand not,<o:p></o:p></i><br />\n<br />\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">How would one teach it?\"<o:p></o:p></i><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-B1SPzF4pn3k/TurUphz2mCI/AAAAAAAAJ_Y/VWcrSed6k40/s1600/imagesCAKH14V8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-B1SPzF4pn3k/TurUphz2mCI/AAAAAAAAJ_Y/VWcrSed6k40/s1600/imagesCAKH14V8.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nOne of the lessons of the Upanishads is that you must regard <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\"the universe as a thought in the mind of the Creator, thereby reducing all discussions of material creation to futility.\" The Upanishads teach that both space and time are endless or infinite. Modern science completely agrees. </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vOs1X7J9ny0/TurS2PpS7vI/AAAAAAAAJ9Y/MXydS9sGulU/s1600/imagesCAS0B2DA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vOs1X7J9ny0/TurS2PpS7vI/AAAAAAAAJ9Y/MXydS9sGulU/s1600/imagesCAS0B2DA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe ancient Maharshis understood the staggering scale of the divine play. Many centuries later the scientific mind still boggles at the scale of creation which makes infinity intelligible. The Rishis clearly perceived that the most fundamental characteristic of this incomprehensible creation was that it was in a perpetual state of movement, flow and change. Lila is a rhythmic play which goes on in endless cycles, the One becoming the many and the many returning to the One.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kGqbQc6qQ2s/TurUhRvuLoI/AAAAAAAAJ_Q/uwp8vuPiVAc/s1600/imagesCAIWKJL2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kGqbQc6qQ2s/TurUhRvuLoI/AAAAAAAAJ_Q/uwp8vuPiVAc/s1600/imagesCAIWKJL2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nModern physics has come to the conclusion that mass is nothing but a form of energy. It would not be an exaggeration to say that the basis of the theory of relativity, and the space-time character of the universe, were perceived by the old Indian Rishis in their advanced stage of spiritual consciousness. In their state of higher consciousness they realized that the ultimate constituents of the universe - energy and mass, particle and wave, - were but different aspects of the same basic process, but the same Oneness which pervaded the entire universe. </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YUC2wSyHp3o/TurW7thY53I/AAAAAAAAKA4/L11yRQnc-gY/s1600/imagesCAT2AKMR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YUC2wSyHp3o/TurW7thY53I/AAAAAAAAKA4/L11yRQnc-gY/s1600/imagesCAT2AKMR.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nToday science has relearned that lesson.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Science, in its most advanced stage, is closer to Vedanta than ever before. <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">The intuition of Indian mystics led them to understand the multidimensional reality and of space-time continuum which is the basis of the modern theory of relativity. </span><o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jId1O5-F4r0/TurSvSdmUdI/AAAAAAAAJ9Q/25gOES-38MA/s1600/imagesCAVQD5WE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jId1O5-F4r0/TurSvSdmUdI/AAAAAAAAJ9Q/25gOES-38MA/s1600/imagesCAVQD5WE.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nIt is in the Upanishads we find all the fundamentals that are central to Hinduism \u2014 the concepts of 'karma' (action), 'samsara' (reincarnation), 'moksha' (nirvana), the 'atman' (soul), and the 'Brahman' (Absolute Almighty). They also set forth the prime Vedic doctrines of self-realization, yoga and meditation.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QBY4Hc_QjgI/TurUTrUt0CI/AAAAAAAAJ_A/sd1Rl7_kd_o/s1600/imagesCAFV1PZK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QBY4Hc_QjgI/TurUTrUt0CI/AAAAAAAAJ_A/sd1Rl7_kd_o/s1600/imagesCAFV1PZK.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe Upanishads are summits of thought on mankind and the universe, designed to push human ideas to their very limit and beyond. They give us both spiritual vision and philosophical argument, and it is by a strictly personal effort that one can reach the truth.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Wy-hwa2rfHk/TurXVyV47KI/AAAAAAAAKBA/94afFoiiwuI/s1600/imagesCA51UDDH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Wy-hwa2rfHk/TurXVyV47KI/AAAAAAAAKBA/94afFoiiwuI/s1600/imagesCA51UDDH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of the oldest and longest of the Upanishads, the <i>Brihadaranyaka ( 1.3.28 ) </i>says: This was my school morning assembly prayer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<strong>\u0950 <span class=\"tooltip\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u0905\u0938\u0924\u094b</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span class=\"tooltip\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span class=\"tooltip\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u0917\u092e\u092f</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span class=\"tooltip\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u0936\u093e\u0928\u094d\u0924\u093f\u0903</span></span> \u0965</strong><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<strong><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot;;\"></span></strong><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Om Asato Maa Sad-Gamaya |<br />\nTamaso Maa Jyotir-Gamaya |<br />\nMrtyor-Maa Amrtam Gamaya |<br />\nOm Shaantih Shaantih Shaantih ||</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"From the unreal lead me to the real! <br />\nFrom darkness lead me to light! <br />\nFrom death lead me to immortality!\"</span></i><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/fiOHTozG3io/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/fiOHTozG3io&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/fiOHTozG3io&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-TMZBwX_wpkE/TurSp9tmy5I/AAAAAAAAJ9I/lA9VxAnkuys/s1600/imagesCAWOV9Q1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-TMZBwX_wpkE/TurSp9tmy5I/AAAAAAAAJ9I/lA9VxAnkuys/s1600/imagesCAWOV9Q1.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThe human being is the central mystery of the universe holding the key to all other mysteries. It was such a science that India sought and found in the Upanishads in an attempt to unravel the mystery of human beings and of consciousness.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4gN_kSLM45Y/TurUNyd7vBI/AAAAAAAAJ-4/39wA3nKnozY/s1600/imagesCAEXRTIV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4gN_kSLM45Y/TurUNyd7vBI/AAAAAAAAJ-4/39wA3nKnozY/s1600/imagesCAEXRTIV.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The purpose of the Vedas was to ensure the true welfare of all beings, worldly as well as spiritually. Before such a synthesis could be achieved, there was a need to penetrate the inner worlds to its depth. This is what the Upanishads did with precision and gave us the science of the self, which helps man leave behind the body, the senses, the ego and all other non-self elements, which are perishable. The Upanishads tell us the great saga of this discovery \u2014 of the divine in the heart of man.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KMmz7MHBFNM/TurUG-1nEYI/AAAAAAAAJ-w/Fnte6hJjRxs/s1600/imagesCA26C7IY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KMmz7MHBFNM/TurUG-1nEYI/AAAAAAAAJ-w/Fnte6hJjRxs/s1600/imagesCA26C7IY.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">These Indian thinkers were not satisfied with their intellectual speculations. They discovered that the universe remained a mystery and the mystery only deepened with the advance of such knowledge, and one of the important components of that deepening mystery is the mystery of man and consciousness. The Upanishads became aware of this truth, which modern science now emphasizes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Bv06qC-16zA/TurUacYqokI/AAAAAAAAJ_I/u--3KynD9m4/s1600/imagesCA55H21C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Bv06qC-16zA/TurUacYqokI/AAAAAAAAJ_I/u--3KynD9m4/s1600/imagesCA55H21C.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the Upanishads we get a glimpse into the workings of the minds of the great Indian thinkers who were unhampered by the tyranny of religious dogma, political authority, pressure of public opinion, seeking truth with single-minded devotion, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>rare in the history of thought. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_goXeclKQt8/TurSg_unlsI/AAAAAAAAJ9A/hx8zIHoK1as/s1600/imagesCAK8S85I.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_goXeclKQt8/TurSg_unlsI/AAAAAAAAJ9A/hx8zIHoK1as/s1600/imagesCAK8S85I.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Max Muller</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> : \"None of our philosophers, including Heraclitus, Plato, Kant, or Hegel has ventured to erect such a spire, never to be frightened by storm or lightnings.\" <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-A77VDY0w56c/TurUAMjd_ZI/AAAAAAAAJ-o/8NwoOePvD3c/s1600/imagesCAKOJTSJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-A77VDY0w56c/TurUAMjd_ZI/AAAAAAAAJ-o/8NwoOePvD3c/s1600/imagesCAKOJTSJ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin: 0.25in 0in;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The physical and mental climate that made it possible is the land of plenty that was India</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They had found leisure and peace to think and ask questions. They had the choice to utilize the leisure either to conquer the outer world or the inner. With their mental gifts, they had turned their mental energies to the conquest of the inner world rather than of the world of matter and life at the sensate level.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TkGvGuOLWkk/TurSbu6nXqI/AAAAAAAAJ84/E_AxQG4Yk2U/s1600/images%252B%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TkGvGuOLWkk/TurSbu6nXqI/AAAAAAAAJ84/E_AxQG4Yk2U/s1600/images%252B%252812%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Upanishads have given us a body of insights that have a universal quality about them and this universality derives from their impersonality. The sages who discovered them had depersonalized themselves in the search for truth. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Unlike modern Western philosophers who lift ideas and patent it in their names. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6VsCOkIhtBI/TurT4z90JdI/AAAAAAAAJ-g/y7LzulgY_eE/s1600/imagesCAM8ZFV9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6VsCOkIhtBI/TurT4z90JdI/AAAAAAAAJ-g/y7LzulgY_eE/s1600/imagesCAM8ZFV9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The rishis wanted to go beyond nature and realize the transcendental nature of man. They dared to take up this challenge and the Upanishads are the unique record of the methods they adopted, the struggles they undertook and the victory they achieved in this astonishing adventure of human spirit. And this is conveyed to us in verses of great resonance power and poetic charm. In seeking the immortal, the Vedic seers conferred the immortality upon the literature that conveyed it.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_Bxuo9EagCQ/TurTw4DRO1I/AAAAAAAAJ-Y/CwtSymK2wmo/s1600/imagesCAFJC6ZO.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_Bxuo9EagCQ/TurTw4DRO1I/AAAAAAAAJ-Y/CwtSymK2wmo/s1600/imagesCAFJC6ZO.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nIn the Upanishads we can study the graceful conflict of thought with thought, the emergence of more satisfactory thought and the rejection and unlearning of inadequate ideas. Hypotheses were advanced and rejected on the touchstone of experience and not at the dictate of a creed. Thus thought forged ahead to unravel the mystery of the world in which we live</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-g_ZejG5X81I/TurQu1RX_1I/AAAAAAAAJ7A/z7r4i1wFDaw/s1600/images+%252811%2529wwwww.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-g_ZejG5X81I/TurQu1RX_1I/AAAAAAAAJ7A/z7r4i1wFDaw/s1600/images+%252811%2529wwwww.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><u>H. <span style=\"color: blue;\">BODHI DHARMA AND SHAOLIN TEMPLE</span></strong><br />\n<br />\nThis is in response to a request from one of my readers 3 months ago--about the 108 Marmas of Kalari.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><strong>Kalaripayattu is NOT a sport.</strong></span> <br />\n<br />\nIt is a LETHAL method of fighting , which is 6000 years old and was introduced to Kerala&nbsp;by Lord Parashurama ( an avatar of Vishnu ) <br />\n<br />\nQuite often we have western fighters coming to Kerala to learn Kalaripayattu , and then after a week they want to fight.<br />\n<br />\nGentlemen, be aware that this form of Kerala Martial art does not leave two men standing. Only one remains--the other is dead, or severely crippled.<br />\n<br />\nLet me digress--<br />\n<br />\nAbout 15 years ago, my ship was going up a South American river. The pilotage was long and tedious, with the river swollen due to floods.<br />\n<br />\nThe pilot was a tall and handsome guy of German descent. He was nice to talk to. <br />\n<br />\nI noticed that his knuckle boneheads were smashed up-- and the tendons displaced into the recesses -- so this means he could punch into concrete slabs without hurting himself. <br />\n<br />\nIn between I had to go down to sort out a machinery problem caused by human carelessness , and by the time I got back on the bridge , I was in a nasty mood.<br />\n<br />\nI resumed my conversation with the pilot-- then I told him \" You appear to be a trained fighter!\"<br />\n<br />\nSo this dude starts off with the degree of the black belt he holds -- etc . And then I could see the inherent arrogance surfacing. <br />\n<br />\nI stopped him when he said \" I can whip anybody on this planet!\" ( the way Mike Tyson had told on TV before ).<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IZzHTK58SlY/Tucq4toD2fI/AAAAAAAAJz4/v6ug7U2TiYY/s1600/imagesCAQFZ9HS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"223\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IZzHTK58SlY/Tucq4toD2fI/AAAAAAAAJz4/v6ug7U2TiYY/s320/imagesCAQFZ9HS.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMy Chief officer and Quarter master were listening to all this in silence. I winked at Chief Officer, took out my key chain from my pocket, and told the pilot to hold it in his hand.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-x2c5WgowPwU/Tucpr_VKM6I/AAAAAAAAJzg/Y18ruRARk5k/s1600/imagesCAGKWCME.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"288\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-x2c5WgowPwU/Tucpr_VKM6I/AAAAAAAAJzg/Y18ruRARk5k/s320/imagesCAGKWCME.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThen I stepped back by about 6 feet , and told him to press the black button on the handle. A small sharp box cutter blade snapped out. I told him \" I know where your jugular vein is-- if I am half the distance closer, it just takes me less than a second to kill you\"<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-t_0zUY0awd8/TucoNU20QcI/AAAAAAAAJzA/j0no2hYlMF4/s1600/imagesCAVLUW7H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-t_0zUY0awd8/TucoNU20QcI/AAAAAAAAJzA/j0no2hYlMF4/s1600/imagesCAVLUW7H.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe pilot's face became white, and my Chief Officer and Quarter Master nearly fainted.<br />\n<br />\nThen I said \" Now press the red button on the side\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-enYBnxS4cUE/Tucoq9kq_JI/AAAAAAAAJzQ/OcgYOwAUKT0/s1600/imagesCAX5CXZ7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-enYBnxS4cUE/Tucoq9kq_JI/AAAAAAAAJzQ/OcgYOwAUKT0/s1600/imagesCAX5CXZ7.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nA compass divider snapped out-- only difference was it had fish hooks at the end.<br />\n<br />\nI told him \" If I decide to be kind and not kill you , then I can make you give any crew member of my ship a blow job on your fuckin' knees for the next 2 hours ! \" <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NJArpOgY6Ns/TucohjDvQ0I/AAAAAAAAJzI/RG6j_HjUe1U/s1600/imagesCAB8LOKO.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"131\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NJArpOgY6Ns/TucohjDvQ0I/AAAAAAAAJzI/RG6j_HjUe1U/s200/imagesCAB8LOKO.jpg\" width=\"200\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAnd then immediately I apologised --told him I am very sorry . <br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n---with an added advise \" Never ever under estimate your opponent \".<br />\n<br />\nThen I instructed my Chief Officer to take my key chain from the pilot and throw it overboard, into the river.&nbsp; It had a plastic handle-- OK Marpol Annex 5 plastic pollution--never mind!<br />\n<br />\nThen I offered him a stiff drink, noticing he needed to steady his nerves &nbsp;. He immediately grabbed the offer.&nbsp; <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pZ2BQXQscgY/VdhQvv7lagI/AAAAAAAA8LI/RYkj2rAV52U/s1600/tumblr_m9cdaEv696m1r9o70s.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pZ2BQXQscgY/VdhQvv7lagI/AAAAAAAA8LI/RYkj2rAV52U/s640/tumblr_m9cdaEv696m1r9o70s.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nHard drinks are NOT allowed on the bridge-- but then here was an extraordinary situation-- which needed an extraordinary solution\" <br />\n<br />\nThe next day my Chief Officer remarked \" Bloody hell, how many times I sat opposite to you peacefully having a chilled beer, &nbsp;with your key chain right in front of me -- you are a dangerous man!\"<br />\n<br />\nI do hope my readers have got the drift-- <span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">Kalaripayattu is NOT a sport!</span><br />\n<br />\nSo what makes me competent to talk on this subject?<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nIn Kerala daughters&nbsp;are sent for dancing and boys are sent for learning Kalripayattu--at a young age. This is a timeless tradition.<br />\n<br />\nDance is graceful dance --not mini skirted and mini pantied cheerleader type jumping around or acrobatics or gymnastics --<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/btnKJO0dUmM/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/btnKJO0dUmM&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/btnKJO0dUmM&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nYou don't get to handle weapons till you are mature.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nAnd only if the Asan ( gurikkal ) feels that you are devoid of arrogance and worth it, only then will he teach you the 108 MARMAS-- or the vital Prana points.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nAll marma point do NOT have the same effect.&nbsp; Some kill instantly ( bindu points ) ,&nbsp; some incapacitate , some immobilise (vaikalyakara ), some give vertigo and loss of sensory ability.<br />\n<br />\nIn some if you leave the invaded object as it is you will survive, if you remove it, you will die.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lVYA4Lf7E5s/TucraixTnWI/AAAAAAAAJ0I/Aflhfj_eSTI/s1600/imagesCA3CLNGT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lVYA4Lf7E5s/TucraixTnWI/AAAAAAAAJ0I/Aflhfj_eSTI/s1600/imagesCA3CLNGT.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nTill then you are literally going through the grind-- the Asan or Guru is in total control of you. You have to do rigorous training for neuro muscular co-ordination , flexibility , stamina and balance of the spirit level in your inner ear cochlea. </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-x_-MJcZaq0s/Tucx1zz4-bI/AAAAAAAAJ0g/rxvvHb7BtQk/s1600/imagesCAS7BDU6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-x_-MJcZaq0s/Tucx1zz4-bI/AAAAAAAAJ0g/rxvvHb7BtQk/s1600/imagesCAS7BDU6.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nAt the end of the daily session is a tedious oil foot massage to stretch the ligaments. Probably it was more to see if you have sustained some injury.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nInitially only wooden weapons are allowed.</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/nM1bcsgx4kg/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/nM1bcsgx4kg&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/nM1bcsgx4kg&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nMind you this teacher-student&nbsp;relationship is a spiritual one , as you have to prostrate and touch his feet everyday, before you enter the Kalari ( arena ).<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uEf-2xk5BXc/TudZNGq2KCI/AAAAAAAAJ2A/QEGdr-D0jr4/s1600/imagesCASWWDU3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"212\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uEf-2xk5BXc/TudZNGq2KCI/AAAAAAAAJ2A/QEGdr-D0jr4/s320/imagesCASWWDU3.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i><span style=\"color: red;\"><b>Modern Reiki of Dr Mikao Usui is taken out of 6000 year old &nbsp;Kalari, the martial art of Kerala, India. &nbsp;You have to lose your fear of injury, pain and death before this \u201chands on\u201d healing can be effective.&nbsp;&nbsp;</b></span></i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"></span><br />\nHe teaches you how to predict an opponents next move- by reading his face and body language.&nbsp; Some amount of&nbsp; Tantra and aura reading is involved here.<br />\n<br />\nPayattu means weapon fight in Malayalam and Sanskrit.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-L_pe7wRTAOc/UwLj8ZSaO3I/AAAAAAAAph0/KSoaj4WmWbA/s1600/kalaripacewgyattu1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"251\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-L_pe7wRTAOc/UwLj8ZSaO3I/AAAAAAAAph0/KSoaj4WmWbA/s1600/kalaripacewgyattu1.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nTill the white man came with their superior fire arms and canons , Kalari warriors protected Kerala from invaders. The first thing the British did was to ban Kalari and imprison all the Kalari teachers.<br />\n<br />\nThe weapon of my choice used to be the Urumi. Now Urumi is a 3 metre long sword, and it is&nbsp;double edged . This serrated tapered lighter and flexible end is saturated with mercury and arsenic poison at the metallurgy stage. You just need to get nicked and draw blood-- you go home and die. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VabwU6vJ2xQ/VdhQ4T69PaI/AAAAAAAA8LQ/aXWekSXrjEU/s1600/extra__weapon__uruRmi_by_sophiablackwoodart-d8ds1el.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VabwU6vJ2xQ/VdhQ4T69PaI/AAAAAAAA8LQ/aXWekSXrjEU/s640/extra__weapon__uruRmi_by_sophiablackwoodart-d8ds1el.jpg\" width=\"604\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nUrumi could be 3 pronged . Wielding a 3 pronged Urumi is a very skilled art. For the end of the sword goes faster that Mach 4 . Mach 1 is the speed of sound or 1221 kilometers per hour.. The crack of a bull whip is a sonic boom.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/d9Qgn52DnBM/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/d9Qgn52DnBM&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/d9Qgn52DnBM&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nIn Kerala bullwhips are used to scare elephants during the training period. <br />\n<br />\nThe accuracy of a trained bull whip wielder is amazing. Last year I saw a circus in Calicut with Russians artistes performing. A gorgeous Russian girl would hold a lit candle on her head and a Russian guy with a long whip would extinguish the flame. Just when we were thinking that this is a fake, he make her hold a apple and sliced it horizontally into two, with her still holding the lower half.
